data-state="closed"><span class="block truncate">ðŸ”¬&nbsp;ULTRA RESEARCH: GOHIGHLEVEL WORKFLOW SYSTEM - COMPLETE ANALYSIS

ðŸ“‹&nbsp;EXECUTIVE SUMMARY

GoHighLevel's Workflow Builder is a&nbsp;visual automation engine&nbsp;that enables no-code automation through:

Triggers&nbsp;(events that start workflows)

Filters&nbsp;(conditions to narrow trigger scope)

Actions&nbsp;(tasks executed sequentially)

Conditions&nbsp;(If/Else branches for logic)

Integrations&nbsp;(external webhooks, APIs, platforms)

For Voice AI automation, GHL provides:

Voice AI-specific triggers&nbsp;(Transcript Generated, Call Status)

Voice AI Custom Actions&nbsp;(real-time webhook calls during live calls)

IVR Actions&nbsp;(Interactive Voice Response for call routing)

Post-call automation&nbsp;(immediate follow-ups based on transcript analysis)

ðŸŽ¤&nbsp;VOICE AI-SPECIFIC FEATURES&nbsp;(Critical for Voice AI Workflows)

1. Voice AI Custom Actions&nbsp;â­â­â­

Purpose:&nbsp;Real-time webhook calls DURING live Voice AI conversation

Key Features:

Trigger on conversation cues&nbsp;- "Check my order status" â†’ triggers API call

POST webhooks with authentication&nbsp;- Bearer tokens, API keys, Basic Auth

Dynamic parameter extraction&nbsp;- AI extracts phone, email, order# from conversation

Real-time response&nbsp;- AI agent speaks the webhook response to caller

Multiple actions per call&nbsp;- Each trigger fires independently

Configuration:

javascript

{

  "name": "Check Order Status",

  "triggerPhrases": [

    "order status",

    "track my order",

    "where is my package"

  ],

  "webhook": {

    "url": "https://your-api.com/orders/status",

    "method": "POST",

    "headers": {

      "Authorization": "Bearer YOUR_TOKEN",

      "Content-Type": "application/json"

    },

    "body": {

      "orderNumber": "{{extracted_order_number}}",

      "phone": "{{caller_phone}}"

    }

  },

  "responseMapping": {

    "status": "order_status",

    "deliveryDate": "estimated_delivery"

  }

}



Use Cases:

CRM lookup during call ("Let me pull up your account...")

Real-time appointment availability check

Order status retrieval

Payment processing mid-call

Custom database queries

Third-party API integrations

2. Transcript Generated Trigger&nbsp;â­â­â­

Purpose:&nbsp;Immediate post-call automation when transcript ready

Available Data:

Full transcript text

Call duration, direction (inbound/outbound)

Caller/recipient phone numbers

Caller location (city, state, zip, country)

Call timestamps (start/end)

Answered by (user name, ID, device)

Call status

Filters:

Call type (Voice AI, IVR, Normal)

Direction (inbound/outbound)

Minimum duration (exclude short calls)

Phone number

User who answered

Advanced Use Cases:

javascript

// Example 1: Keyword-based routing

IF transcript contains "interested in premium"

  â†’ Tag as "Hot Lead"

  â†’ Assign to senior sales rep

  â†’ Send high-priority notification



// Example 2: Sentiment analysis

Pass transcript to GPT-4

  â†’ Analyze sentiment (positive/neutral/negative)

  â†’ If negative: Alert customer success team

  â†’ If positive: Request review



// Example 3: Data extraction

Extract: email, company name, pain points from transcript

  â†’ Update contact custom fields

  â†’ Create opportunity with extracted data

  â†’ Trigger personalized follow-up email



3. IVR Integration

Purpose:&nbsp;Route calls to Voice AI agents based on caller input

IVR Actions for Voice AI:

Gather Input&nbsp;- Get caller selection (press 1 for sales, 2 for support)

Play Message&nbsp;- "Please hold while I connect you to our AI assistant..."

Connect to Call&nbsp;- Route to Voice AI agent or human

Conditional Routing&nbsp;- Route based on business hours, caller history, VIP status

Example IVR â†’ Voice AI Flow:

text

Caller dials â†’ IVR Answers

  â†’ "Press 1 for Sales, 2 for Support"

  â†’ Caller presses 1

  â†’ Connect to Voice AI Sales Agent

  â†’ Voice AI handles qualification

  â†’ If qualified: Transfer to human sales rep

  â†’ If not qualified: Voice AI schedules follow-up



4. Voice AI Outbound Calling&nbsp;(Workflow Action)

Purpose:&nbsp;Trigger Voice AI to make outbound calls from workflows

Parameters:

Agent ID

Phone number to call

Call objective/goal

Custom parameters to pass to agent

Fallback actions if no answer

Use Cases:

Appointment reminders (automated calls 24 hours before)

Lead follow-up (call new leads within 5 minutes)

Payment reminders (call overdue invoices)

Survey calls (post-purchase satisfaction)

Re-engagement (call inactive customers)

ðŸ—ï¸&nbsp;WORKFLOW BUILDER ARCHITECTURE

Core Components:

Triggers&nbsp;- Entry point (1+ per workflow)

Filters&nbsp;- Narrow trigger conditions

Actions&nbsp;- Sequential tasks

Conditions&nbsp;(If/Else) - Branching logic

Wait Steps&nbsp;- Time delays

Goal Events&nbsp;- Early exit points

Workflow Execution:

text

Trigger Fires

  â†“

Apply Filters (optional)

  â†“

Contact enters workflow

  â†“

Action 1 executes

  â†“

Action 2 executes

  â†“

If/Else Condition (optional)

  â”œâ”€ YES path â†’ Action 3

  â””â”€ NO path â†’ Action 4

  â†“

Wait Step (optional)

  â†“

Goal Event check (optional)

  â”œâ”€ Goal met â†’ Exit workflow

  â””â”€ Goal not met â†’ Continue

  â†“

Remaining actions execute

  â†“

Workflow complete



Advanced Features:

Split Testing&nbsp;- A/B test different paths

Arrays&nbsp;- Manipulate data collections

Custom Code&nbsp;- JavaScript/Python for complex logic

Go To&nbsp;- Jump to other workflows

Drip Mode&nbsp;- Control flow rate

Text Formatter&nbsp;- Data manipulation

Webhooks&nbsp;- External integrations

AI Prompts&nbsp;- GPT-powered decisions

   â””â”€ Filter: Days before event

   â”œâ”€ Trigger phrases

   â”œâ”€ Dynamic parameters

   â””â”€ Response mapping

  â”œâ”€ Date comparison

  â”œâ”€ Tag exists/doesn't exist

8. TECHNICAL IMPLEMENTATION



Use React with:

- React Flow library for node-based interface

- Zustand for state management

- React Hook Form for configuration forms

- TailwindCSS for styling

- Lucide React for icons



Data Structure:



interface Workflow {

id: string;

name: string;

status: 'draft' | 'published';

trigger: TriggerNode;

nodes: (ActionNode | ConditionNode)[];

connections: Connection[];

}

interface TriggerNode {

id: string;

type: 'transcript-generated' | 'call-status' | ...;

filters: Filter[];

position: {x: number; y: number};

}

interface ActionNode {

id: string;

type: 'send-email' | 'add-tag' | 'ai-prompt' | ...;

config: Record&lt;string, any&gt;;

position: {x: number; y: number};

}

interface ConditionNode {

id: string;

type: 'if-else';

condition: {

field: string;

operator: 'contains' | 'equals' | 'greater_than' | ...;

value: any;

};

yesBranch: string[]; // node IDs

noBranch: string[]; // node IDs

position: {x: number; y: number};

}

- Test webhook with sample data

- Response preview

- Parameter extraction simulation



Call Flow Simulator:

- Test workflow with simulated Voice AI call

- Step through each node

- View data at each step

- Validate logic before going live



10. VALIDATION &amp; ERROR HANDLING



Workflow Validation:

- Ensure trigger is configured

- Check all actions have required fields

- Validate condition logic

- Warn about orphaned nodes

- Check for infinite loops



Error States:

- Highlight invalid nodes in red

- Show error messages in configuration

- Prevent publishing with errors

- Suggest fixes for common issues

DATA FLOW &amp; CUSTOM VALUES</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Custom Value Picker integration:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Access to Transcript Generated data:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ Full transcript text</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ Call duration, direction</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ Caller phone, location</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ Timestamps</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â””â”€ User who answered</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Contact fields (all standard + custom)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Opportunity data</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Appointment data</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Custom values from previous actions</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">6. WORKFLOW TEMPLATES FOR VOICE AI</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Pre-built templates:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”œâ”€ "New Lead Voice AI Follow-Up"</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”‚  â””â”€ Trigger: Form Submit â†’ Voice AI Call â†’ SMS Confirmation</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”œâ”€ "Appointment Reminder Voice AI"</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”‚  â””â”€ Trigger: Custom Date â†’ Voice AI Call â†’ Update Status</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”œâ”€ "Transcript Analysis &amp; Routing"</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”‚  â””â”€ Trigger: Transcript Generated â†’ GPT Analysis â†’ Route to Team</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”œâ”€ "Failed Call Retry Sequence"</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â”‚  â””â”€ Trigger: Call Status = Missed â†’ Wait â†’ Retry Call</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">â””â”€ "Post-Call Lead Qualification"</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">   â””â”€ Trigger: Transcript Generated â†’ If/Else on Keywords â†’ Tag &amp; Assign</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">7. UI/UX REQUIREMENTS</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Visual Design:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Dark theme with VAPI-style aesthetic (#00ffa3 accents)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Node color coding:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ Triggers: Blue</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ Actions: Green</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ Conditions: Orange</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â””â”€ Wait/Delays: Purple</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Hover states with action buttons (edit, delete, duplicate)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Drag handles for connections</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Right-click context menus</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Keyboard shortcuts (Delete, Ctrl+C/V, Ctrl+Z)</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Configuration Modals:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Slide-in panels for node configuration</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Form validation with error messages</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Dropdown selectors for all options</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Custom value picker with search</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Test button for webhooks</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Preview mode for templates</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Workflow Management:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Save/Load workflows</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Draft/Published status toggle</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Workflow naming and description</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Version history (optional)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Export/Import JSON</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Clone workflow functionality</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">8. TECHNICAL IMPLEMENTATION</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Use React with:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- React Flow library for node-based interface</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Zustand for state management</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- React Hook Form for configuration forms</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- TailwindCSS for styling</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Lucide React for icons</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Data Structure:</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">interface Workflow {</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">id: string;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">name: string;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">status: 'draft' | 'published';</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">trigger: TriggerNode;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">nodes: (ActionNode | ConditionNode)[];</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">connections: Connection[];</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">}</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">interface TriggerNode {</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">id: string;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">type: 'transcript-generated' | 'call-status' | ...;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">filters: Filter[];</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">position: {x: number; y: number};</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">}</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">interface ActionNode {</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">id: string;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">type: 'send-email' | 'add-tag' | 'ai-prompt' | ...;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">config: Record&lt;string, any&gt;;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">position: {x: number; y: number};</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">}</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">interface ConditionNode {</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">id: string;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">type: 'if-else';</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">condition: {</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">field: string;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">operator: 'contains' | 'equals' | 'greater_than' | ...;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">value: any;</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">};</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">yesBranch: string[]; // node IDs</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">noBranch: string[]; // node IDs</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">position: {x: number; y: number};</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">}</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">text</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">9. VOICE AI-SPECIFIC FEATURES</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Transcript Analysis Panel:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Show sample transcript in configuration</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Highlight keywords that match conditions</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Test conditions against sample data</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Suggest relevant actions based on transcript content</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Voice AI Custom Action Builder:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Visual webhook configuration</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Test webhook with sample data</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Response preview</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Parameter extraction simulation</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Call Flow Simulator:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Test workflow with simulated Voice AI call</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Step through each node</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- View data at each step</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Validate logic before going live</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">10. VALIDATION &amp; ERROR HANDLING</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Workflow Validation:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Ensure trigger is configured</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Check all actions have required fields</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Validate condition logic</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Warn about orphaned nodes</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Check for infinite loops</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Error States:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Highlight invalid nodes in red</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Show error messages in configuration</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Prevent publishing with errors</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Suggest fixes for common issues</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">===========================================</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">DELIVERABLES:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">===========================================</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Create a single-file HTML application with:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">1. Complete workflow builder interface</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">2. All Voice AI triggers and actions</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">3. Working drag-and-drop functionality</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">4. Configuration modals for each node type</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">5. Sample Voice AI workflow templates</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">6. Export functionality (JSON)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">7. Dark theme with modern styling</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Focus on these Voice AI workflow patterns:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Post-call automation (transcript analysis)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Real-time call actions (custom webhooks)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Call outcome routing (if/else based on results)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Multi-step follow-up sequences</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">- Failed call retry logic</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">The builder should feel like GoHighLevel's workflow editor but be optimized specifically for Voice AI agent automation scenarios.</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">ðŸŽ&nbsp;BONUS: KEY VOICE AI WORKFLOW PATTERNS</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Pattern 1: Intelligent Lead Routing</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">text</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Trigger: Transcript Generated (Call Duration &gt; 60s)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â†“</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Action: AI Prompt (GPT-4)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â””â”€ Analyze transcript for buying intent</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â†“</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">If/Else: Intent Score &gt; 7</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”œâ”€ YES: </span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”‚   â”œâ”€ Add Tag "Hot Lead"</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”‚   â”œâ”€ Assign to Senior Sales Rep</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â”‚   â””â”€ Send Internal Notification (high priority)</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â””â”€ NO:</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">      â”œâ”€ Add Tag "Nurture"</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">      â””â”€ Add to Email Drip Campaign</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Pattern 2: Appointment Booking Confirmation</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">text</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Trigger: Appointment Status = Booked</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â†“</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">Action: Voice AI Outbound Call</span><br><span data-lexical-text="true">  â””â”€ "Hi, this is [Agent]. <h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="executive-summary">Executive Summary</h2>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">GoHighLevelâ€™s Workflow Builder is a sophisticated visual automation engine purpose-designed for no-code business process automation, with a growing focus on supporting advanced Voice AI agent workflows. This document synthesizes the entire catalog of available triggers, actions, Voice AI specific capabilities, UI/UX requirements, node-based editor patterns, error/validation principles, and industry-leading technical implementation detailsâ€”packaged for blueprinting a modern, Cursor-ready Workflow Builder project.</p>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="system-overview--core-principles">System Overview &amp; Core Principles</h2>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>1. Visual, Node-Based Workflow Canvas</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Infinite drag-and-drop grid for node positioning (React Flow recommended)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Node types: Triggers, Actions, Filters, Conditions, Wait, Goal, etc.</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Smooth connection lines, auto-layout options</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Minimap, zoom/pan, and fit-to-screen navigation</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Color and icon schemes to distinguish node types</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>2. Workflow Structure Components</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Triggers: Start workflows on events (full catalog below)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Filters: Refine when triggers should act</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Actions: Task nodes executed in sequence</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">If/Else Conditions &amp; Branching: Visual logic controls with colored connections (YES/NO)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Wait/Delay steps, Goal Events</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Data references: Pass data between nodes; access contact fields, transcript details, opportunity data, etc.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>3. Voice AIâ€“Optimized Workflow Support</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Voice AI drivers: Transcript analysis, live call hooks, post-call automations</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Dedicated triggers/actions for Voice AI (see below)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Real-time webhooks with parameter extraction from calls</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Outbound call automation and IVR support</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Post-call workflows using transcript sentiment, keyword, entity extraction</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="complete-trigger-node-catalog-with-filters--voice">Complete Trigger Node Catalog (with Filters &amp; Voice AI Use Cases)</h2>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">

<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">See attached document for the full catalog of trigger categories and sample Voice AI use cases, covering Contact, Event, Appointment, Opportunity, Affiliate, Course, Payment, Shopify, IVR, Social Media, and Community triggers.</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Each trigger includes available filters and relevant Voice AI automation patterns.</p>
</li>

<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="complete-action-node-catalog-with-parameter-exampl">Complete Action Node Catalog (with Parameter Examples &amp; Voice AI Ties)</h2>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Refer to attached catalog, documenting 14 main categories: Contact, Communication, Send Data, Internal Tools, Workflow AI, Eliza, Appointment, Opportunity, Payment, Marketing, Affiliate, Course, IVR, and Community Actions.</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Parameter and field details outlined for each, with sample Voice AI automations.</p>

<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="voice-aispecific-architectures">Voice AIâ€“Specific Architectures</h2>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>A. Real-Time Voice AI Custom Actions</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Custom actions invoke POST webhooks mid-conversation</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Dynamic parameter mapping from conversation: order #, caller phone, etc.</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Response mapping, authentication (Bearer, API Key, Basic Auth)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Each trigger can have multiple actions, each fires independently</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Example config: see original JSON sample</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>B. Transcript-Generated Automation</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Immediate workflow step triggered as soon as transcript is available</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Access full transcript, call metadata, outcomes, duration</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Filters: call type, direction, keywords, min. duration</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Use cases: auto-tag sales calls, sentiment analysis, extract data to update CRM, follow-up marketing</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>C. IVR Integration</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Gather Input: Voice or DTMF input for menu routing</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Play Message, Connect to Call, End Call, Record Voicemail</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Route to Voice AI agent per input value; handle conditional logic for business hours, VIP, etc.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>D. Outbound Voice AI Calling</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Trigger bulk or one-off calls from workflow actions</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Pass agent, goal, targeted phone, fallback routing</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Use for reminders, lead follow-up, payment, survey, reactivation calls</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="uiux-requirements">UI/UX Requirements</h2>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>A. Canvas &amp; UX Patterns</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Drag-and-drop workflow canvas (React Flow baseline)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Node palette/sidebar with search/filter; drag nodes to canvas</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Colored node categories: Triggers (blue), Actions (green), Conditions (orange), Wait (purple), etc.</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Mini-map for overview, zoom-in/out and pan controls</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Right-click menus/contextual action bars on nodes</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Slide-in or modal panels for node configuration</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Node badges for filter counts, error/warning indication</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Node-level edit (edit, delete, duplicate)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Draggable connection ends for visual linking</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>B. Node Configuration Experience</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Dedicated configuration modal/panel per node</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Type-specific options: Triggers (filter logic), Actions (parameter mapping, test/preview), Conditions (selector, AND/OR branching)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Intelligent field validation: required fields, correct types</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Data/variable picker for references (transcript fields, custom fields, context data, etc.)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">AI Assistant button: Open sidebar with context-sensitive help, examples, validation tips</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>C. Workflow Management UI</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Workflow list: Create, clone, version, status (draft/published), export (JSON), import</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Template gallery: Save/load common Voice AI workflows</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Preview mode: Simulate/test workflow with sample data</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Runner function: Executes nodes in order, displays step/edge transition</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Change history and autosave</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>D. Error Handling &amp; Validation</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Errors highlighted on nodes and in global/persistent error bar</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Inline field validation with actionable feedback</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Contextual suggestions: AI-powered tips, help doc links</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Support for step-level summaries, error aggregation bar</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Accessibility: Proper ARIA, logical tab order, screen reader support, icons+color indicators</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="technical-stack-recommended-proven-in-industry">Technical Stack (Recommended, Proven in Industry)</h2>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>React</strong> for main UI</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>React Flow</strong> for node-based workflow interface</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>Zustand</strong> for state management</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>shadcn-ui</strong> &amp; <strong>TailwindCSS</strong> for styling components</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>Lucide React</strong> for consistent iconography</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>ELKjs</strong> for automatic layouting/graph organization</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>React Hook Form</strong> for managing forms/config modals</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="data-structures">Data Structures</h2>

<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="advanced-features">Advanced Features</h2>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>AI Assistance:</strong> Contextual help for each node, config tip sidebar, real-world examples</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>Split Testing:</strong> A/B split node, track outcomes down different branches</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>Arrays &amp; Custom Coding:</strong> Node for handling lists/arrays; custom Python/JS node for advanced logic</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>Goal Event Nodes:</strong> Branch/exit based on end-state achieved</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>Drip Mode:</strong> Rate limiting, batched delay options for sequences</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="patterns--example-templates">Patterns &amp; Example Templates</h2>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">See the attached document for four core Voice AI workflow templates: Intelligent Lead Routing, Appointment Booking, Failed Call Recovery, Real-Time Order Status.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="error-design-best-practices">Error Design Best Practices</h2>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Use clear color and icon cues on nodes and in sidebars</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Position error summaries close to the problem step, with persistent area for ongoing issues</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Provide next-action suggestions directly on error card</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Present error logic that scales with branching and deep flows</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Ensure accessibility (keyboard navigation, ARIA, readable icons)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<blockquote>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">This document provides the entire requirements and structural blueprint to build a GoHighLevel Voice AIâ€“optimized workflow builder in Cursor or any modern React environment.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="executive-summary">Executive Summary</h2>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">GoHighLevelâ€™s Workflow Builder is a sophisticated visual automation engine purpose-designed for no-code business process automation, with a growing focus on supporting advanced Voice AI agent workflows. This document synthesizes the entire catalog of available triggers, actions, Voice AI specific capabilities, UI/UX requirements, node-based editor patterns, error/validation principles, and industry-leading technical implementation detailsâ€”packaged for blueprinting a modern, Cursor-ready Workflow Builder project.</p>
<hr class="bg-subtle h-px border-0" node="[object Object]">
<h2 class="mb-2 mt-4 font-display font-semimedium text-base first:mt-0 md:text-lg [hr+&amp;]:mt-4" id="system-overview--core-principles">System Overview &amp; Core Principles</h2>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>1. Visual, Node-Based Workflow Canvas</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Infinite drag-and-drop grid for node positioning (React Flow recommended)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Node types: Triggers, Actions, Filters, Conditions, Wait, Goal, etc.</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Smooth connection lines, auto-layout options</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Minimap, zoom/pan, and fit-to-screen navigation</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Color and icon schemes to distinguish node types</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>2. Workflow Structure Components</strong></p>
<ul class="marker:text-quiet list-disc">
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Triggers: Start workflows on events (full catalog below)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Filters: Refine when triggers should act</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Actions: Task nodes executed in sequence</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">If/Else Conditions &amp; Branching: Visual logic controls with colored connections (YES/NO)</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Wait/Delay steps, Goal Events</p>
</li>
<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Data references: Pass data between nodes; access contact fields, transcript details, opportunity data, etc.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2"><strong>3. Voice AIâ€“Optimized Workflow Support</strong></p>

<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Voice AI drivers: Transcript analysis, live call hooks, post-call automations</p>

<li class="py-0 my-0 prose-p:pt-0 prose-p:mb-2 prose-p:my-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:pt-0 [&amp;&gt;p]:mb-2 [&amp;&gt;p]:my-0">

<p class="my-2 [&amp;+p]:mt-4 [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:inline-block [&amp;_strong:has(+br)]:pb-2">Post-call workflows using transcript sentiment, keyword, entity extraction</p>
